***балалайка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:балалайка.html>балала́йка</a> (17501)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">балаба́йка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balabájka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from onomatopoeic <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">балабай-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balabaj-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">балабо́нить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balabónitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">балагу́рить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balagúritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бала́кать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balákatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баланда.html>бала́нда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">balánda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баланда.html>бала́нды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баланда.html>бала́нды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баланда.html>бала́нд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> skillygalee</li>

***баланс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баланс.html>бала́нс</a> (8906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***балансировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:балансировать.html>баланси́ровать</a> (17949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">balancieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балансировать.html>баланси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">balansírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сбаланси́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to balance, to keep one's balance</li>
<li>to balance, to equipoise</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***балахон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:балахон.html>балахо́н</a> (14428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. Formerly unsuccessfully derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">بالا جامه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bālā jāme</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">upper dress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>. May be related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бала́хтать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baláxtatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">splash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бала́хтаться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baláxtatʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балахон.html>балахо́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">balaxón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балахон.html>балахо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балахон.html>балахо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балахон.html>балахо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> loose peasant overgarment made of sackcloth or twill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> loose-fitting robe</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>балбе́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">balbés</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балбес.html>балбе́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балбес.html>балбе́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балбес.html>балбе́сов</a></b>)

***балда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>балда</a> (14885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>балда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">baldá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балда.html>балды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балда.html>балды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балда.html>ба́лд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sledgehammer</li>
<li><i>m and f</i> blockhead, dolt, dunderhead</li></ol>

***балдеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:балдеть.html>балде́ть</a> (22482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>балда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baldá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:балдеть.html>балде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">baldétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обалдеть.html>обалде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stop thinking clearly, to take leave of one's senses</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get/be high;</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have fun; to lead a fun life, to be idle</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллон.html>балло́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ballón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллон.html>балло́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллон.html>балло́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллон.html>балло́нов</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллончик.html>балло́нчик</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баллончик.html>балло́нчик</a> (28181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллон.html>балло́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ballón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллончик.html>балло́нчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ballónčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллончик.html>балло́нчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллончик.html>балло́нчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллончик.html>балло́нчиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gas cartridge containing incapacitating liquid, for self-defense (e.g. pepper spray)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баллон.html>балло́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ballón</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gas or liquid canister</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>баловать</a> (11952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">баловати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balovati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flatter, to heal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*badlovati</i>. Per Vasmer, cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">balováti</i> and probably not to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">बाल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bāla</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">kid, infant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>балова́ть</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>ба́ловать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">balovátʹ</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bálovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избаловать.html>избалова́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избаловать.html>изба́ловать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побаловать.html>побалова́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побаловать.html>поба́ловать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to indulge, to spoil, to pet, to pamper</li>
<li>to give a treat</li></ol>

***баловаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баловаться.html>баловаться</a> (11619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>балова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловаться.html>балова́ться</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловаться.html>ба́ловаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">balovátʹsja</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bálovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to frolic, to play about, to fool around, to get up to monkey tricks
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баловаться.html>балу́йся</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne balujsja!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't be naughty/mischievous!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to amuse oneself <i>(with)</i>, to dabble <i>(in/at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:баловаться.html>баловаться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:живопись.html>жи́вописью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>balovatʹsja</b> žívopisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dabble at/in painting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to indulge <i>(in)</i>, to treat oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:баловаться.html>баловаться</a></b> чайко́м</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>balovatʹsja</b> čajkóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to treat oneself to some tea; have tea</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:баловаться.html>баловаться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выпивка.html>вы́пивкой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>balovatʹsja</b> výpivkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to indulge in drinking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have sex, to fool about <i>(with)</i>, to mess <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>балова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">избалова́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izbalovátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побаловаться.html>побалова́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobalovátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***баловень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баловень.html>ба́ловень</a> (29330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>балова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловень.html>ба́ловень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bálovenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловень.html>ба́ловня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловень.html>ба́ловни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловень.html>ба́ловней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> favorite, darling, pet, coddle, cosset <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a person or animal especially cherished, indulged or spoiled</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:баловень.html>ба́ловень</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьбы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bálovenʹ</b> sudʹbý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lucky (person)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mischievous child</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">mischievous child</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">баловни́к</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">balovník</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>шалу́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šalún</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баловство.html>баловство́</a> (17873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>балова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловать.html>ба́ловать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bálovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловство.html>баловство́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">balovstvó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баловство.html>баловства́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<ol><li>naughtiness, mischievousness</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бамбук.html>бамбу́к</a> (19881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">bambu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">bambu</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бамбук.html>бамбу́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bambúk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бамбуковый.html>бамбу́ковый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bambúkovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bamboo
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бамбуковый.html>бамбу́ковая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bambúkovaja</b> mébelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>bamboo</b> furniture</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бамбуковый.html>бамбу́ковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bambúkovyj</b> medvédʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">giant panda</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>bamboo</b> bear</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***банан.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>банан</a> (10901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">banane</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">banana</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolof_language" class="extiw" title="w:Wolof language">Wolof</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wo">banaana</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>бана́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">banán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:банан.html>бана́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:банан.html>бана́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:банан.html>бана́нов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:банановый.html>бана́новый</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бана́нчик</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>banana <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tree or fruit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>joint of marijuana
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>  “Бананы  | Bananas | ”, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leningrad_(band)" class="extiw" title="w:Leningrad (band)">Leningrad</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́йте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:банан.html>бана́нов</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:марихуана.html>марихуа́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнца</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́йте</a>!!!</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dájte <b>banánov</b>, marixuány sólnca dájte!!!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Give me some bananas, of marijuana, honey give me some!!!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бандитский.html>банди́тский</a> (9620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бандит.html>банди́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bandít</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бандитский.html>банди́тский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bandítskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thug, bandit, highwayman</li>
<li>thug's, bandit's, highwayman's</li>
<li>like a bandit, thug, or highwayman</li></ol>
